
-----title
永泰（永福） (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f2eaa02de2a2415597cdfbdddf3d0158_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f2eaa02de2a2415597cdfbdddf3d0158");'><span id='f2eaa02de2a2415597cdfbdddf3d0158_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1101')">1091-1101年</a>，1-11岁</div><div id='f2eaa02de2a2415597cdfbdddf3d0158' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年1月1日</a>　是年正月初一出生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1100')">1092-1100年</a>　少居家乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　少居家乡。母亡。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='49b9a799c19a48149c18b3eb15d67c07_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("49b9a799c19a48149c18b3eb15d67c07");'><span id='49b9a799c19a48149c18b3eb15d67c07_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>，29岁</div><div id='49b9a799c19a48149c18b3eb15d67c07' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年6月</a>　至故乡永福，得乃祖手迹，刻诸石，并祭扫祖母刘氏墓，为文以祭。作品：《祭祖母彭城郡夫人刘氏墓文》<div id='poem_1236695' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236695' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236695?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭祖母彭城郡夫人刘氏墓文</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和元年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236695")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236695_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236695'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236695'>昔我先祖，未取科第，于时夫人，始作之配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236695_comment'></div>儒生穷愁，想见中馈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236695_comment'></div>逮生多男，室则已继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236695_comment'></div>同穴送终，是为林氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236695_comment'></div>宜夫人宅，独厝兹地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236695_comment'></div>荒山深林，樵牧不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236695_comment'></div>历数十载，父老不记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236695_comment'></div>有孙爰归，发其久翳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236695_comment'></div>闻诸里闾，叹息出涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236695_comment'></div>生虽不享，死亦子贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236695_comment'></div>彭城之封，象服炜炜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236695_comment'></div>酾酒割牲，用示幽贲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236695_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1236695_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年7月</a>　在乡期间，曾谒郑侠，结识僧隆老。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年11月</a>　十一月，离乡返京。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='173699beb601479b8d2150d0bbac28bf_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("173699beb601479b8d2150d0bbac28bf");'><span id='173699beb601479b8d2150d0bbac28bf_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>，31岁</div><div id='173699beb601479b8d2150d0bbac28bf' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>是年，因方腊起义，避乱还永福，有文祭西禅隆老。作品：《祭西禅隆老文》<div id='poem_1236694' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236694' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236694?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭西禅隆老文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236694")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236694_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236694'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236694'>谨以香烛、伊蒲塞之馔，致祭于某人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236694_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236694_comment'></div>顷之识师，临平始归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236694_comment'></div>退处彼庵，钟山其西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236694_comment'></div>粤时宣和己亥季夏，圜顶加冠，以笑以语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236694_comment'></div>伤今念古，师适我同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236694_comment'></div>由尔定交，有孚于中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236694_comment'></div>别曾几何，乱起方腊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236694_comment'></div>克勘南征，爰奋北伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236694_comment'></div>四海横溃，我还旧庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236694_comment'></div>忧患荐罹，独师悯诸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236694_comment'></div>师生丙申，阅世烂久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236694_comment'></div>吾闽有禅，师必称首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236694_comment'></div>百年老榕，忽仆道周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236694_comment'></div>此木其坏，职师是忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236694_comment'></div>我来哭师，本安用哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236694_comment'></div>聊慰后人，示激颓俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236694_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1236694_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>又为西禅隆老作赞。作品：《西禅隆老海印大师赞》<div id='poem_1236676' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236676' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236676?labeling=true' target='_blank'>西禅隆老海印大师赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236676")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236676_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236676'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236676'>扬子江心，饱经波浪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236676_comment'></div>临平山上，看尽风光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236676_comment'></div>蓦然唱个还乡曲，来坐海上古道场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236676_comment'></div>其圜机转物也，山河大地不离掌握；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236676_comment'></div>其辩口谈天也，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1236676", 1236676, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>邪魔外道</span>为之胆碎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236676_comment'></div>知我者谓我逢场作戏，不知我者谓我拖泥带水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236676_comment'></div>请看父母未生时，只这面目何曾是？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236676_comment'></div>咄！</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1236676_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='4424c2ad1fff4481a4e0c0a0ee042ce4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4424c2ad1fff4481a4e0c0a0ee042ce4");'><span id='4424c2ad1fff4481a4e0c0a0ee042ce4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>，46岁</div><div id='4424c2ad1fff4481a4e0c0a0ee042ce4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年4月26日</a>　在永福，有《荐拔水陆功德疏》<br /></div><div class='label1' id='1eea28b6dabf41749bc4eb05a2a20f42_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1eea28b6dabf41749bc4eb05a2a20f42");'><span id='1eea28b6dabf41749bc4eb05a2a20f42_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年</a>，55岁</div><div id='1eea28b6dabf41749bc4eb05a2a20f42' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年2月</a>　二月，在永福与李文中宴饮，有词。作品：《怨王孙》（霁雨天迥）<div id='poem_108193' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108193' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/108193?labeling=true' target='_blank'>怨王孙/忆王孙<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_108193")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_108193_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_108193'>绍兴乙丑春二月既望，李文中置酒溪阁。日暮雨过，尽得云烟变态，如对营丘著色山。坐客有歌怨王孙者，请予赋其情抱，叶子谦为作三弄，吹云裂石，旁若无人，永福前此所未见也。老子于此，兴复不浅</div><div id='poem_preface_108193_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_108193'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_108193'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_108193", 108193, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>霁雨</span>天迥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_108193_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_108193'>平林烟暝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_108193_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_108193'>灯闪沙汀，水生钓艇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_108193_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_108193'>楼外柳暗谁家。<div id='poem_sentence_3_108193_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_108193'>乱昏鸦。<div id='poem_sentence_4_108193_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_108193'>相思怪得今番甚。<div id='poem_sentence_5_108193_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_108193'>寒食近。<div id='poem_sentence_6_108193_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_108193'>小砑鱼笺信。<div id='poem_sentence_7_108193_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_108193'>屏山交掩，微醉独倚阑干。<div id='poem_sentence_8_108193_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_108193'>恨春寒。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_108193_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年</a>　是年，李文中任满，有诗送别。作品：《送李文中主簿受代归庭闱》<div id='poem_108012' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108012' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/108012?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送李文中主簿受代归庭闱</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_108012")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_108012_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_108012'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_108012'>豹隐犹遮雾，鸾栖遂及瓜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_108012_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_108012'>绿林方在境，䌽服径还家。<div id='poem_sentence_1_108012_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_108012'>世路久来险，人情何用嗟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_108012_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_108012'>胸中自丘壑，乐处是生涯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_108012_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_108012'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_108012_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

临漳

-----title
南昌
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年</a>　在豫章问句法于徐俯，并与江西诗派成员结诗社唱和。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年</a>　是年仍在豫章，与徐俯、吕本中等结社唱和。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='a337624fb24a45e0b644288dbc13f2ca_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a337624fb24a45e0b644288dbc13f2ca");'><span id='a337624fb24a45e0b644288dbc13f2ca_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年1月</a>　正月到达豫章，为家书以训子孙。作品：《芦川豫章观音观书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年2月</a>　与徐俯、洪刍游，二人皆为之题跋。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年2月</a>　自豫章，下白沙，阻风吴城山，有词。作品：《满江红•自豫章阻风吴城山作》<div id='poem_108263' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108263' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/108263?labeling=true' target='_blank'>满江红 自豫章阻风吴城山作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_108263")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_108263_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_108263'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_108263'>春水迷天，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_108263", 108263, "Clauses/1/Comments/1")'>桃花浪</span>、几番风恶。<div id='poem_sentence_0_108263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_108263'>云乍起、远山遮尽，晚风还作。<div id='poem_sentence_1_108263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_108263'>绿卷芳洲生杜若。<div id='poem_sentence_2_108263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_108263_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_108263'>寒犹在，衾偏薄。<div id='poem_sentence_5_108263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_108263'>肠欲断，愁难著。<div id='poem_sentence_6_108263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_108263'>倚<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_8_108263'>寒食清明都过却。<div id='poem_sentence_8_108263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_108263'>最怜轻负年时约。<div id='poem_sentence_9_108263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_108263'>想小楼、终日望归舟，人如削。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_108263_comment'></div></div><div -----title
开封
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2c844937d1094a5c803e741c4817568e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2c844937d1094a5c803e741c4817568e");'><span id='2c844937d1094a5c803e741c4817568e_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年1月</a>　初春，在东都，有词。作品：《菩萨蛮•政和壬辰东都作》<div id='poem_108246' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108246' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/108246?labeling=true' target='_blank'>菩萨蛮<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>政和壬辰东都作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_108246")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_108246_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_108246'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_108246'>黄莺啼破纱窗晓。兰缸一点窥人小。<div id='poem_sentence_0_108246_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_108246'>春浅锦屏寒。麝煤金博山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_108246_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　夏间，与陈与义、吕本中、苏庠叔侄在汴京，以诗唱和。作品：《跋苏诏君楚语后》<div id='poem_1236659' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236659' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236659?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋苏诏君楚语后<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二十七年五月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236659")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236659_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236659'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236659'>《风》、《雅》之变，始有《离骚》，与《诗》六义相表里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236659_comment'></div>比兴虽多，然卒皆正而不淫，哀而不怨，宜乎古今推屈、宋为盟主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236659_comment'></div>后之数子，如《九怀》、《九叹》、《七发》、《七启》之类，著意摹仿，未免重复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236659_comment'></div>姑置工拙如何，大槩开卷使人易倦，良由轨辙一律，窃窃然追逐前贤步武间，心殚力疲，不能跳脱翰墨畦径，良可恨尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236659_comment'></div>观吾养直所作，摅发己意，肆而不拘，凡所形容，不蕲合于屈、宋，政自超诣，殆不可企及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236659_comment'></div>此章赠别从周者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236659_comment'></div>顷在东都，一日，陈去非、吕居仁诸公同予避暑资圣阁，以「二仪清浊还高下，三伏炎蒸定有无」分韵赋诗，会者适十四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236659_comment'></div>从周诗颇佳，为诸公印可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236659_comment'></div>然则阮嗣宗喜仲容，又常曰「吾不如与阿戎谈」，方之养直，惓惓如此，不为过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236659_comment'></div>从周后养直数载云亡，其子庭藻有志古学，手抄《离骚》，成诵不辍，且求为乃翁跋所藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236659_comment'></div>顾家有哲匠，但熟读数百过，何患落笔不名世耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236659_comment'></div>芦川老人书于槜李弭棹亭中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236659_comment'></div>丁丑仲夏望日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1236659_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　有词与王及之唱和。作品：《浣溪沙•王仲时席上赋木樨》<div id='poem_108229' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108229' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a -----title
南平（延平）

class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_108140")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_108140_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_108140'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_108140'>飞观插雕梁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_108140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_108140'>凭虚起、缥缈五云乡。<div id='poem_sentence_1_108140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_108140'>对山滴翠岚，两眉浓黛，水分双派，满眼波光。<div id='poem_sentence_2_108140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_108140'>曲栏干外，汀烟轻冉冉，莎草细茫茫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_108140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_108140'>无数钓舟，最宜烟雨，有如图画，浑似潇湘。<div id='poem_sentence_4_108140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_108140'>使君行乐处，秦筝弄哀怨，云鬓分行。<div id='poem_sentence_5_108140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_108140'>心醉一缸春色，满座疑香。<div id='poem_sentence_6_108140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_108140'>有天涯倦客，尊前回首，听彻伊川，恼损柔肠。<div id='poem_sentence_7_108140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_108140'>不似碧潭双剑，犹解相将。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_108140_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='69cc0c81c0a74927ae7785d1a889d9d0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("69cc0c81c0a74927ae7785d1a889d9d0");'><span id='69cc0c81c0a74927ae7785d1a889d9d0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>，50岁</div><div id='69cc0c81c0a74927ae7785d1a889d9d0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>　过延平，有《山桂庵铭》<div id='poem_1236687' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236687' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236687?labeling=true' target='_blank'>山桂庵铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236687")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236687_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236687'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236687'>晋安刘公华即延平官舍西麓，诛茅结庐，面山旁桂，地不踰丈，而尽挹胜览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236687_comment'></div>真隐居士过焉，命曰「山桂庵」，取小山丛桂之句也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236687_comment'></div>因为作铭，铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1236687'>眼界贵宽，心地贵閒，耳根贵静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236687_comment'></div>刘子结庐，畏此简书，虽吏云隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236687_comment'></div>山光苍苍，溪水泱泱，是用适性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236687_comment'></div>旁据桂丛，秋芬扬风，俯视奔竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236687_comment'></div>谁为赏音，与时浮湛，期则有命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236687_comment'></div>凡厥后来，优哉游哉，顺受其正。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1236687_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

星子

<div class='label1' id='e7450cf2c0824079b28a18fdfd13c8e6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e7450cf2c0824079b28a18fdfd13c8e6");'><span id='e7450cf2c0824079b28a18fdfd13c8e6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>，30岁</div><div id='e7450cf2c0824079b28a18fdfd13c8e6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　春，陪陈了翁游庐山，逗留累月，常与之商榷古今治乱成败，有诗纪游。作品：《游庐山》<span class='inlineComment2'>（是诗不见于芦川本集，《全宋诗》第31册19931页题作《游庐山》）</span><div id='poem_107900' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_107900' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/107900?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游庐山</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_107900")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_107900_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_107900'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_107900'>古木寒藤挽我住，身非靖节谁能留。<div id='poem_sentence_0_107900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_107900'>多惭不及鸾溪水，长向山前山后流<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋曾季狸《艇斋诗话》）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_107900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_107900'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_107900_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

无锡

href='/Writing/108083?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉送李叔易博士被召赴行在所</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_sentence_11_108083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_108083'>难兄难弟实间出，直欲并驾仍齐驱。<div id='poem_sentence_12_108083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_108083'>承明入谒一见决，三迁故事登元枢。<div id='poem_sentence_13_108083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_108083'>整顿乾坤赖公等，我病只合山林居。<div id='poem_sentence_14_108083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_108083'>残年正尔甚易与，不过二顷邻一区。<div id='poem_sentence_15_108083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_108083'>平生故人半廊庙，老僧何患无门徒。<div id='poem_sentence_16_108083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_108083'>与君痛饮遽成别，努力强饭供时须。<div id='poem_sentence_17_108083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_108083'>男儿富贵亦细事，否泰相反分贤愚。<div id='poem_sentence_18_108083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_108083'>酒酣起舞莫作恶，行矣自爱千金躯。<div id='poem_sentence_19_108083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_108083'>本朝再造旧基业，速拯涂炭疲氓苏。<div id='poem_sentence_20_108083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_108083'>勿令毫发有遗恨，文章尔雅华国犹其馀。<div id='poem_sentence_21_108083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_108083'></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_108083_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
杭州

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年</a>　旋至杭州，寓居西湖，游宝藏寺有诗。作品：《丁未岁春过西湖宝藏寺》<div id='poem_108062' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108062' class='poemTitle DetailSwitch("000b8288feda4a5bb52b6a1718b305c4");'><span id='000b8288feda4a5bb52b6a1718b305c4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: gray;'>▪</span>是年，坐作词送胡铨追赴临安大理寺，削籍除名。被抄家，词多被搜去，散佚甚多。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>出狱后，作词抒愤，以旷达之笔写其不甘屈服、无所畏惧之怀。作品：《水调歌头•罢秩后漫兴》<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b48af9326a504220af00b366b6464010_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b48af9326a504220af00b366b6464010");'><span id='b48af9326a504220af00b366b6464010_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年</a>，65岁</div><div id='b48af9326a504220af00b366b6464010' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在临安，与胡仔游。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>是年芦川在临安，并跋《江天暮雨图》作品：《跋江天暮雨图》<br /></div><div class='label1' id='11ee3a44d63044a4836cf1492ef1d563_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("11ee3a44d63044a4836cf1492ef1d563");'><span id='11ee3a44d63044a4836cf1492ef1d563_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1159')">1157-1159年</a>，67-69岁</div><div id='11ee3a44d63044a4836cf1492ef1d563' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年9月</a>　九月，陈正同除刑部侍郎，有贺启。作品：《贺陈都丞除刑部侍郎启》<div id='poem_1236619' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236619' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236619?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺陈都丞除刑部侍郎启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236619")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236619_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236619'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236619'>显膺中制，荣陟贰卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236619_comment'></div>公朝登用于正人，羽仪增重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236619_comment'></div>清议依归于直节，班列生辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236619_comment'></div>举善类以起予，觉斯民而向化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236619_comment'></div>仰窥亲擢，果属老成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236619_comment'></div>窃以世禄象贤，源流盖有所自；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236619_comment'></div>异材间出，被遇贵得其时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236619_comment'></div>求忠臣于孝子之门，采令誉于名德之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236619_comment'></div>理应一揆，进或殊涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236619_comment'></div>粤若了堂真儒长雄，谏垣耆旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236619_comment'></div>平生刚烈，论奸邪于交结之初；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236619_comment'></div>先见著明，力排击于变更之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236619_comment'></div>去国而分甘百谪，笃信奚疑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236619_comment'></div>尊君而独奋孤忠，始终尽瘁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236619_comment'></div>躬履践不欺闇室，视富贵如彼浮云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236619_comment'></div>旷千古以靡俦，有死无贰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236619_comment'></div>舍百身而莫赎，卒老于行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236619_comment'></div>推天定胜人之机缄，观否极泰来之卦象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236619_comment'></div>然好还者虽迟亦验，顾忍穷者唯恐弗坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236619_comment'></div>宜在子孙，复兴门户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236619_comment'></div>恭惟某官资性端亮，胸次坦夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236619_comment'></div>通六艺以经纶，循五常而允蹈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236619_comment'></div>夙奉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1236619", 1236619, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>过庭之训</span>，克遵良冶之传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236619_comment'></div>佩服话言，罔愆先志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236619_comment'></div>发挥事业，是似乃翁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236619_comment'></div>受知负扆之明，爰拜司寇之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236619_comment'></div>想对扬于密勿，深启沃于渊衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236619_comment'></div>云龙之会难逢，日月之光必照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236619_comment'></div>聊烦持橐，伫庆秉钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236619_comment'></div>某衰退何能，嵚崎可笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236619_comment'></div>蚤侍先生之杖屦，转头垂四十年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236619_comment'></div>与闻远识之蓍龟，倒指无二三子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236619_comment'></div>题评甚宠，词翰永藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236619_comment'></div>自怜忧患之馀龄，获睹衣冠之盛事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236619_comment'></div>伸吾道英灵之气，慰前人忠愤之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236619_comment'></div>敢希拔茅以茹连，徒诵茂松而柏悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236619_comment'></div>私相欣幸，倍万等伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236619_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1236619_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　羁寓西湖之上，结识周德友及张孝祥。作品：《苏养直诗帖跋尾六篇》<div id='poem_1236656' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236656' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236656?labeling=true' target='_blank'>苏养直诗帖跋尾六篇</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236656")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236656_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236656'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236656'>往在豫章，问句法于东湖先生徐师川，是时洪刍驹父、弟琰玉父、苏坚伯固、子庠养直、潘淳子真、吕本中居仁、汪藻彦璋、向子諲伯恭，为同社诗酒之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236656_comment'></div>予既冠矣，亦获攘臂其间，大观庚寅辛卯岁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236656_comment'></div>九人者，宰木久已拱矣，独予华发苍颜，羁寓西湖之上，始及识德友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236656_comment'></div>一日，出示养直翰墨凡六大轴，各索题跋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236656_comment'></div>适连宵雨作春泥，良是中原禁烟天气，篝灯拥火，追记旧游，悄悄不能寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236656_comment'></div>乘醉为书，且念向来社中人物之盛，予虽有愧群公，尚幸强健云<span class='inlineComment2'>（右甲卷。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236656_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1236656'>士之出处隐显，各行其志，顾始终一节如何耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236656_comment'></div>尧舜之世，不废巢、由，是故楚狂接舆、长沮、桀溺、荷筱丈人辈，垂名万古，不必皆策勋钟鼎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236656_comment'></div>历代信史，未有无隐逸者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236656_comment'></div>异时董狐复出，诛奸谀于既往，则养直之幽光愈彰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236656_comment'></div>玉局老仙发明在前，罗浮真人印可在后，中间数十年，略未尝为尘埃所污，亦要用吾曹辄下语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236656_comment'></div>德友意则勤矣，尚复奚言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236656_comment'></div>姑以甲乙次第其卷，辄归诸巾衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236656_comment'></div>芦川老隐书<span class='inlineComment2'>（右乙卷。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236656_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1236656'>亡友养直神情萧散，仪矩雍容，自是贵公子，而识度超诣，照了世法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236656_comment'></div>英妙时已甘心山泽之臞，故词翰似其为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236656_comment'></div>良由家世名德之后，平生履践，追配前哲，晚乃力辞召聘，高卧不起，老于丘园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236656_comment'></div>盖此事素定于胸中，非一时矫激沽誉者，宜乎仙去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236656_comment'></div>虽无罗浮金丹，其意已在云烟灭没间久矣，黄真人者那得不一引手耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236656_comment'></div>芦川老隐云<span class='inlineComment2'>（右丙卷。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236656_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1236656'>养直未见东坡时，出语落笔便脱去翰墨畦径，自有一种风味，真所谓飘飘然凌云之志，所以受知于东坡先生，许其为神仙中人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236656_comment'></div>德友所藏诗词，多是《后湖集》中所未有，要当流传墨本，用贻好事者，吾德友终能深袭独秘耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236656_comment'></div>如《木犀词》末句「身到十洲三岛，心游万壑千岩」，是岂轩冕所能笼络也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236656_comment'></div>平生大节如此，纵非仙去，自足以高一世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236656_comment'></div>此语可为知者道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236656_comment'></div>芦川老隐云<span class='inlineComment2'>（右丁卷。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236656_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1236656'>养直此轴十数帖，皆为德友往返尺书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236656_comment'></div>其间情话，无非输肺肝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236656_comment'></div>虽甚匆遽时，行书小草，浓澹欹正，初若信手，而笔意俱到，句中有味，览之使人忘倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236656_comment'></div>至于论虞尤佐人物：「挂冠神武之兴，此举固清；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236656_comment'></div>然二十四考中书令者，复何人斯」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236656_comment'></div>此论可垂方来，不当只付之戏笑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236656_comment'></div>芦川老隐云<span class='inlineComment2'>（右戊卷。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236656_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1236656'>养直二十三帖作一轴，笔意圆熟，词采精明，如珠走槃，略无定势，而璀璨夺目，光彩射人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236656_comment'></div>反复寻绎，沈著痛快，诚不在杨少师之下，李西台所不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236656_comment'></div>德友尤宜宝惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236656_comment'></div>此老不妄许可人，而乃拳拳如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236656_comment'></div>观其《卜居帖》中所谓「山色云涛四环，正当山水佳处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236656_comment'></div>此段果成，异日遂为烟波主人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236656_comment'></div>公若肯入社，当分半座」，在他人殆未易得此语也，德友其能忘怀耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236656_comment'></div>顷年江左亲旧说养直别业在澧阳，三两载必一往检过，经行佳处，所至痛饮，未尝不与人倾倒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236656_comment'></div>篙师打鼓发船，张帆呼风，每苦养直醉卧江上酒垆边，鼾息如雷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236656_comment'></div>高标远韵，当求之晋、宋间，此生那复见斯人耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1236656_comment'></div>芦川老隐云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1236656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1236656'><span class='label'>按：</span>右己卷。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1236656_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　羁寓西湖，与张孝祥游，有跋文。作品：《跋张安国所藏山水小卷》<div id='poem_1236662' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236662' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236662?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋张安国所藏山水小卷</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236662")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236662_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236662'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236662'>世所谓胸次有丘壑者，穷而士，达而公卿，其心未尝须臾不住烟云水石间，又况如吾宗安国得友人把玩短轴，褾而藏之，每出以示诸好事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236662_comment'></div>虽乌帽黄尘，汩没困顿，开卷便觉万里江山在眼界中，可想蜀僧为同舍郎周旋落笔时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236662_comment'></div>然则安国不忘故旧，风味如此，胸次可知矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1236662_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　羁寓西湖。为人作墓志铭。作品：《晋安黄夫人墓志铭》<div id='poem_1236689' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236689' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236689?labeling=true' target='_blank'>晋安黄夫人墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二十八年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236689")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236689_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236689'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236689'>有宋处士郑君德称之室黄氏，台州黄岩县尉讳待问之长女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236689_comment'></div>黄，乡先生也，家世晋安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236689_comment'></div>夫人自幼聪慧过人，事亲诚孝，先生夫妇素钟爱之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236689_comment'></div>择所宜配，年二十，归处士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236689_comment'></div>治家渐渐有条理，岁时祀事，必躬蠲洁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236689_comment'></div>驭臧获辈，宽猛适当，得其欢心，未尝施鞭扑，唯以善言诲训之，率就规矩，不怒而威，咸耻有过失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236689_comment'></div>十五年中，安贫自乐，顺适处士之意，颇如德耀事伯鸾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236689_comment'></div>内外姻党，无间疏戚，闻夫人之风，靡不钦慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236689_comment'></div>岁在癸巳夏四月，处士殁于大父旧庐，夫人时年未四十，持丧甚严，诸孤累累然方龆龀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236689_comment'></div>夫人非特能守其志，且虑郊居从师匪便，亟斥卖奁具，得舍数椽，直郡庠之左，俾儿曹朝夕尊所闻见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236689_comment'></div>盖不待三迁，果皆业儒，夫善师孟母若夫人者鲜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236689_comment'></div>绍兴辛未春正月，以寿终，享年七十八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236689_comment'></div>后七年戊寅岁某月某日，岊举其柩，合葬于处士墓，是为怀安县钦德里文山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236689_comment'></div>男三人：长曰岊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236689_comment'></div>次曰岳，早卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236689_comment'></div>季曰冈，尝预乡荐，不禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236689_comment'></div>女亦未嫁而夭，今独岊存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236689_comment'></div>孙男二人，曰庚、曰育，皆为士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236689_comment'></div>孙女三人，长适进士陈炳文，馀在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236689_comment'></div>岊雅尚不群，无心进取，以翰墨游公卿，养母尽孝，人喜馈之，用助甘旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236689_comment'></div>与予别八九年矣，三遣书白葬期，必欲求予铭其母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236689_comment'></div>每请愈坚，义不可辞，乃为之铭曰<span class='inlineComment2'>（铭阙）</span>：</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1236689_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年</a>　春日，居临安西湖，与郭世模等游。作品：《郭从范示及张安国诸公酬唱辄次原韵》<div id='poem_108035' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108035' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/108035?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郭从范示及张安国诸公酬唱辄次严韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_108035")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_108035_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_108035'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_108035'>登楼乘暇日，唤客共浇愁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_108035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_108035'>春去花犹发，阴浓雨未休。<div id='poem_sentence_1_108035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_108035'>和诗真冷澹，得句总风流。<div id='poem_sentence_2_108035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_108035'>能遣西邻老，殊无陋巷忧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_108035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_108035'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_108035_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

宜兴

-----title
湖州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='794962690a4e4a6c926919c3ee8e4af7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("794962690a4e4a6c926919c3ee8e4af7");'><span id='794962690a4e4a6c926919c3ee8e4af7_link' style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，避难至吴兴，目睹时事，作词抒愤。作品：《石州慢•己酉秋吴兴舟中作》<div id='poem_108148' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108148' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_0_108148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_108148'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_108148", 108148, id='poem_sentence_1_108148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_108148'>夜帆风驶，满湖烟水苍茫，菰蒲零乱秋声咽。<div id='poem_sentence_2_108148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_108148'>梦断酒醒时，倚危樯清绝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_108148_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_108148'>心折。<div id='poem_sentence_4_108148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_108148'>长庚光怒，群盗纵横，逆人猖獗。<div id='poem_sentence_5_108148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_108148'>欲挽天河，一洗中原膏血。<div id='poem_sentence_6_108148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_108148'><span class='link' "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>塞垣</span>祗隔长江，唾壶空击悲歌缺。<div id='poem_sentence_7_108148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_108148'>万里想龙沙，泣孤臣吴越。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_108148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_108148'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(108148)'>评注</a><span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　是年春，寓居湖州千金村，与葛胜仲父子从游唱和，生活贫困，尝绝粮，并形于歌咏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　与公泽处士往还，剧谈时事，有诗。作品：《次韵奉公泽处士》<div id='poem_107973' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_107973' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a -----title
宁波（庆元府）

id='poem_sentence_1_108086'>杀气西北来，遗毒成僭窃。<div id='poem_sentence_1_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_108086'>议和其祸胎，割地亦覆辙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_108086'>傥从种将军，用武寨再劫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_108086'>不放匹马回，安得两宫说。<div id='poem_sentence_4_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_108086'>巍巍开国初，真宰创鸿业。<div id='poem_sentence_5_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_108086'>一统包八荒，受降临观阙。<div id='poem_sentence_6_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_108086'>并州稍稽命，骈头亟膏钺。<div id='poem_sentence_7_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_108086'>于今何势殊，天王狩明越。<div id='poem_sentence_8_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_108086'>诸镇本藩翰，楚破阖城血。<div id='poem_sentence_9_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_108086'>翠舆欲东巡，蹈海计愈切。<div id='poem_sentence_10_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_108086'>诏下散百司，恩许保妻妾。<div id='poem_sentence_11_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_108086'>瞻彼廉陛尊，孰与壮班列。<div id='poem_sentence_12_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_108086'>肉食知谋身，未省肯死节。<div id='poem_sentence_13_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_108086'>检校舆地图，宁复见施设。<div id='poem_sentence_14_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_108086'>三吴素轻浮，伤弓更心折。<div id='poem_sentence_15_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_108086'>四顾皆惊波，苍黄共呜咽。<div id='poem_sentence_16_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_108086'>维兹艰危秋，贫士转疏拙。<div id='poem_sentence_17_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_108086'>明年谷增贵，贤愚罔分别。<div id='poem_sentence_18_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_108086'>何处置我家，患在建午月。<div id='poem_sentence_19_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_108086'>故山盍早归，岂忧践霜雪。<div id='poem_sentence_20_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_108086'>作意海边来，初非事干谒。<div id='poem_sentence_21_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_108086'>责我卖屋金，流言尚为孽。<div id='poem_sentence_22_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_108086'>汪公德甚大，游说情激烈。<div id='poem_sentence_23_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_108086'>力救归装贫，一洗肝肺热。<div id='poem_sentence_24_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_108086'>如公趋急难，正似古豪侠。<div id='poem_sentence_25_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_108086'>行藏道甚明，亲养志先决。<div id='poem_sentence_26_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_108086'>去矣茅三间，无问衣百结。<div id='poem_sentence_27_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_108086'>他时期卜邻，此日尤惜别。<div id='poem_sentence_28_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_108086'>请以兄事公，尺书未宜缀。<div id='poem_sentence_29_108086_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_108086'></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_108086_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>赵次张有诗来问候，故芦川以诗答之，有怀归诗。作品：《次韵赵次张见遗之什韵》<div id='poem_107964' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_107964' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/107964?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次赵次张见遗之什韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_107964")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_107964_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_107964'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_107964'>海边游子日思归，新句劳君更置规。<div id='poem_sentence_0_107964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_107964'>莫问人间多贝锦，正如天上有参旗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_107964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_107964'>寄书只欲凭黄耳，去路谁能畏赤眉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_107964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_107964'>定与故巢猿鹤老，此生无愧北山移。<div id='poem_sentence_3_107964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_107964'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_107964_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
德清
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='62f160a9e225415ebd7be8e71134ea58_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("62f160a9e225415ebd7be8e71134ea58");'><span id='62f160a9e225415ebd7be8e71134ea58_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年12月</a>　年底，举家避乱重返吴兴，过德清白彪村访沈琯。作品：《过白彪访沈次律有感十六韵》<div id='poem_108077' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108077' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_108077'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_108077'>天骄毒中原，国势苦日削。<div id='poem_sentence_0_108077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_108077'>一为虚声摇，颠沛几失脚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_108077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_108077'>翠华栖海隅，此戏亦太虐。<div id='poem_sentence_5_108077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_108077'>坐令临安城，开关犹白著。<div id='poem_sentence_6_108077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_108077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_108077'>岂无英雄人，戴宋心未薄。<div id='poem_sentence_9_108077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_108077'>有如沈使君，忠义等筹略。<div id='poem_sentence_10_108077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_108077'>始终誓复仇，志愿久已确。<div id='poem_sentence_11_108077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_108077'>浮家来水村，避乱畏矰缴。<div id='poem_sentence_12_108077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_108077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_108077'>吾衰世无用，鼓勇徒矍铄。<div id='poem_sentence_15_108077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_107941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_107941'>药囊能济物，龟策少知音。<div id='poem_sentence_1_107941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1236614_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下建中兴之业，将恢复于旧邦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236614_comment'></div>求共理之良，亦广搜于属籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236614_comment'></div>臣敢不抚绥千里，谨防贼盗之凭陵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236614_comment'></div>经画一城，更赖山河之险固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236614_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1236614_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

福州

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　是年挂冠前后有诗。作品：《西峡行》<div id='poem_108075' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108075' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_108075")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_108075_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_108075'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_108075'>西峡门东晚潮上，涛头驾风高数丈。<div id='poem_sentence_0_108075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_108075'>绝江艇子更扬帆，风水相吞两岸壮。<div id='poem_sentence_1_108075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_108075'>中流荡潏思虑深，欲济未竟愁夕阴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_108075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_108075'>贾客胡商数航海，忍死射利诚何心。<div id='poem_sentence_3_108075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_108075'>不如遵陆困舆皂，九折羊肠复相恼。<div id='poem_sentence_4_108075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_108075'>下临湍濑千仞渊，胥靡轻生履危道。<div id='poem_sentence_5_108075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_108075'>我曹过计常私忧，垂堂之戒宁自尤。<div id='poem_sentence_6_108075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_108075'>经营一饱亦细事，世乱畏涂归罢休。<div id='poem_sentence_7_108075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_108075'>少年新进真儿剧，浪喜功名不量力。<div id='poem_sentence_8_108075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_108075'>杀身无补误朝廷，天下英雄古难得。<div id='poem_sentence_9_108075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_108075'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_108075_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　是年挂冠归来之初有词。作品：《蝶恋花（窗暗窗明昏又晓）》<div id='poem_108280' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108280' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_108280'>百岁光阴，老去难重少。<div id='poem_sentence_1_108280_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_108280'>四十归来犹赖早。<div id='poem_sentence_2_108280_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_108280'>浮名<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_108280", 108280, id='poem_sentence_7_108280_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_108279' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108279' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/108279?labeling=true' "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>打坐</span>安闲好。<div id='poem_sentence_3_108279_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_108279'>败意常多如意少。<div id='poem_sentence_4_108279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_108279'>著甚来由，入闹寻烦恼。<div id='poem_sentence_5_108279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年1月28日</a>　正月二十八日，里人辛炳为之题跋。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年4月</a>　翟汝文自翰林学士承旨、左中大夫知制诰拜参知政事，有贺启。作品：《贺翟参政启》<div id='poem_1236618' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236618' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236618?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺翟参政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236618")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236618_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236618'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236618'>祗奉明纶，聿参魁柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236618_comment'></div>朝廷增重，繄政事之得人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236618_comment'></div>夷夏耸观，盖德威之足畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236618_comment'></div>窃以天启豪杰，必有用而乃生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236618_comment'></div>时际艰危，非大贤而罔济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236618_comment'></div>古今共贯，治乱殊科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236618_comment'></div>傥功业每成于无心，则进退自然而可度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236618_comment'></div>奋身不顾，处君臣一体之间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236618_comment'></div>直道是行，陋左右游谈之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236618_comment'></div>凡登庸者审皆若此，彼朋附者亦何能为！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236618_comment'></div>恭惟某官经术通以佐王，推先儒之领袖；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236618_comment'></div>文章掞而华国，具先辈之典型。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236618_comment'></div>历事三朝，驰声四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236618_comment'></div>妙弥纶于胸次，当相中兴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236618_comment'></div>斡造化于笔端，合居上宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236618_comment'></div>虽负英伟不群之气，常存正直在位之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236618_comment'></div>明目张胆而启沃滋多，正笏垂绅而折冲未艾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236618_comment'></div>载安社稷，恢复舆地之山河；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236618_comment'></div>一洗乾坤，大明普天之日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236618_comment'></div>永作元老，昭示奇勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236618_comment'></div>某罪戾孤踪，流离末路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236618_comment'></div>曾预登门之旧，莫陪贺厦之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236618_comment'></div>举世皆惊，公为苍生而果起；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236618_comment'></div>吾徒相庆，象占君子以汇征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236618_comment'></div>佩服题评，尤加喜抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236618_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1236618_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年5月30日</a>　五月三十日，在福州与友人为文祭邓肃。作品：《诸公祭邓正言文》<div id='poem_1236690' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236690' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236690?labeling=true' target='_blank'>诸公祭邓正言文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年5月30日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236690")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236690_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236690'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236690'>维绍兴二年岁次壬子五月庚申朔，三十日己丑，友人宇文师瑗、张世才、王时、张宇林、杨休、王传、苏籀、余良弼、黄丰、洪蘖、朱松、冯至游、吴叔虎、朱称、李议之、张元干等，谨以清酌庶羞之奠，致祭于亡友正言邓子志宏之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236690_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236690_comment'></div>吾志宏负卓越不羁之才，骋纵横无穷之辩，夫岂不能揣摩捭阖以巧速化，抑岂不能趑趄嗫嚅以容悦苟贱？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236690_comment'></div>雅欲正色而立朝，率由直道而事君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236690_comment'></div>始也风刺，名重诸生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236690_comment'></div>几中奇祸，坐为谏臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236690_comment'></div>耻卖友以自售，宁甘心而守贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236690_comment'></div>故其放斥流离，一寓意于杯酒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236690_comment'></div>悲歌慷慨，时托兴于诗文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236690_comment'></div>浇胸中块垒不平之气，同世间陆沉未遇之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236690_comment'></div>是身虽诎，此道则信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236690_comment'></div>或窃笑以技穷，固多相期乎器远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236690_comment'></div>水莫改于万折，金益坚于百鍊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236690_comment'></div>议论人主之前，周旋天下之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236690_comment'></div>皆吾子所优为，忽盖棺而不见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236690_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236690_comment'></div>子有老母，病久未痊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236690_comment'></div>夕不解衣，药必手煎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236690_comment'></div>积忧成病，反丧盛年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236690_comment'></div>母乃哭子，彼苍者天！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236690_comment'></div>想英姿兮如在，聆妙语兮阒然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236690_comment'></div>邈楚些之不招兮，谅蜕去而为飞仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236690_comment'></div>谁抚诸孤，养其华颠？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236690_comment'></div>心折涕陨，尚复忍言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236690_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉，尚享！</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1236690_comment'></div></div></div><br ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年6月</a>　是年居福州，六月，有诗贺李纲生日。作品：《李丞相生朝三首》《李丞相纲生朝三首》<div id='poem_108060' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108060' class='poemTitle ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年6月</a>　秦梓以直秘阁提点福建刑狱公事，芦川与游，并有词唱和。作品：《采桑子•奉和秦楚材使君荔枝词》<div id='poem_108174' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108174' class='poemTitle id='poem_sentence_1_108061'>我独忧患馀，几为死生隔。<div id='poem_sentence_1_108061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_108061'>相逢忽眼明，照影俱头白。<div id='poem_sentence_4_108061'>如何功名心，一旦乃冰释。<div id='poem_sentence_4_108061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_108061'>卖药真徉狂，穿云忘迁谪。<div id='poem_sentence_5_108061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_108061'>不然蔬笋肠，宁无瘴烟色。<div id='poem_sentence_6_108061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_108061'>良由火枣成，内景充尺宅。<div id='poem_sentence_7_108061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_108061'>下视陋九州，槐安等称国。<div id='poem_sentence_8_108061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_108061'>绝怜蛮触争，亦复弄兵革。<div id='poem_sentence_9_108061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_108061'>乱来更多事，老去觉世窄。<div id='poem_sentence_10_108061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_108061'>归欤桃花源，斑衣作儿剧。<div id='poem_sentence_11_108061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_108061'>此乐人所稀，今我那能得。<div id='poem_sentence_12_108061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_108061'>他时南山南，寄书北山北。<div id='poem_sentence_13_108061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_108061'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_108061_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>　初春，与吕本中等从游唱和。作品：《信中居仁叔正皆有诗访梅于城西而独未暇载酒分付老拙其敢不承》<div id='poem_108087' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108087' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/108087?labeling=true' target='_blank'>信中居仁叔正皆有诗访梅于城西而独未暇载酒分付老拙其敢不承</a><span /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_108087_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_108087'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_108087'>关山往岁曾冰裂，跋马平坡千树雪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_108087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_108087'>疏枝冷蕊最撩人，雪后生香微带月。<div id='poem_sentence_1_108087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_108087'>醉中不数长短亭，狐裘拥鼻风前醒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_108087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_108087'>十年丧乱岂记忆，一见新诗心目惊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_108087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_108087'>平生公辈真豪友，意气相投共杯酒。<div id='poem_sentence_4_108087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_108087'>祇今流落天南端，怅望中原莫回首。<div id='poem_sentence_5_108087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_108087'>及身强健频看梅，此花到眼春光催。<div id='poem_sentence_6_108087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_108087'>玉人风味正清绝，但欠雪月相徘徊。<div id='poem_sentence_7_108087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_108087'>欲访城西寻醉语，竹篱茅舍知何许。<div id='poem_sentence_8_108087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_108087'>携壶藉草傥不嗔，便与此花长作主。<div id='poem_sentence_9_108087_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_108087'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_108125_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年9月9日</a>　重九日，有词。作品：《虞美人》（菊坡九日登高路）<div id='poem_108272' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_108081'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_108081'>孤云乘天风，飞入海上山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_108081_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_108081_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年1月</a>　在鼓山有诗送言上人。作品：《送言上人往见径山老十四韵》<div id='poem_108090' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108090' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/108090?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送言上人往见径山老十四韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年1月）</span><span class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_108090_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_108090'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_108090'>忽辞鼓山行，便作径山去。<div id='poem_sentence_0_108090_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_108090'>道人孤飞云，腰包咄嗟具。<div id='poem_sentence_1_108090_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_108090'>两边兄弟间，杨岐一条路。<div id='poem_sentence_2_108090_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_108090'>禅许众人参，院要大家住。<div id='poem_sentence_3_108090_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_108090'>无是亦无非，何喜复何怒。<div id='poem_sentence_4_108090_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_108160_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_108160'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_108160'>神水华池，汞铅凝结，虎龙往来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_108160_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_108160'>问子前午后，阳销阴长，自然炉鼎，何用安排。<div id='poem_sentence_1_108160_comment'></div></div><div "poem_title_107991")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_107991_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_107991'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_107991'>淮<span class='inlineComment2'>（排印本作湖）</span>海元龙公辈流，何劳老手镇方州。<div id='poem_sentence_0_107991_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_107991'>雍容行色自登览，邂逅故人仍倡酬。<div id='poem_sentence_1_107991_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_107991'>眼界早惊云子熟，官期能为荔枝留。<div id='poem_sentence_2_107991_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_107991'>临分莫话中原事，想见家山只梦游。<div id='poem_sentence_3_107991_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年6月10日</a>　居福州。六月，李纲寿辰，有诗庆贺。作品：《李丞相生朝》<div id='poem_108060' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108060' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_108060'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_108060'>柱史生周室，仙源谱系崇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_108060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_108060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_108060'>梦求终作楫，猎卜果非熊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_108060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_108060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_108060'>社稷攲倾际，乾坤震荡中。<div id='poem_sentence_6_108060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_108060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_108060'>相印机衡重，兵权号令通。<div id='poem_sentence_12_108060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_107935' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_107935' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/107935?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代上折枢彦质生朝二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 id='poem_sentence_4_107948_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　为折彦质文作跋。作品：《跋折仲古文》<div id='poem_1236647' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236647' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236647?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋折仲古文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236647")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236647_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236647'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236647'>晋郝隆为蛮府参军，有「娵隅跃清池」之句，娵隅，鱼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236647_comment'></div>唐顾况作《闽囝》诗，有「囝别郎罢」之句，郎罢，父也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236647_comment'></div>今折丈傲睨万物，游戏笔端，而富丈印可之，如「悒󰇣」二字，是亦古人馀意耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236647_comment'></div>然考诸《方言》，谓使为杀，当用杀礼之杀，以去声呼之，庶几近似。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236647_comment'></div>若乃曰柴，政恐两公一时听讹尔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1236647_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　秋间，陪李纲游鼓山，钱申伯亦同游，有诗唱和。作品：《再和李丞相游山》<div id='poem_107955' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_107955' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年2月</a>　居福州。二月，游雪峰山，时知福州折彦质离任，以诗送其行。作品：《次折枢留题雪峰韵》<div id='poem_107963' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_107963' class='poemTitle id='poem_sentence_1_107963'>故人容野老，胜践<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>见新诗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_107963_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年8月12日</a>　有跋赵文祖贫士图文。作品：《跋赵祖文贫士图后》<div id='poem_1236646' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236646' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236646?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋赵祖文贫士图后<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴九年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年8月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236646")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236646_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236646'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236646'>晋、宋间人物风流，如陶渊明环堵萧然，不蔽风日，短褐穿结，箪瓢屡空，卧北窗下，凉风时至，自谓羲皇上人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236646_comment'></div>此诗独不显姓字，要是当时隐君子耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236646_comment'></div>抑自况也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236646_comment'></div>贫者士之常，胸次所养果厚，必无寒饿憔悴色，故能安于青松白云之下，而操孤鸾别鹤之音，优哉游哉，聊以卒岁，宜其渊明愿留而保岁寒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236646_comment'></div>向使望尘雅拜者稍知金谷园中竟不免祸败，讵肯相率以谄事人耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236646_comment'></div>绍兴己未中秋前三夕，庵居不寐，风雨骤来，悽然有感，篝灯起坐，取无量所示祖文《东方贫士图》作跋，迟明归之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1236646_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年8月15日</a>　与赵无量游，有跋文。作品：《跋山居图》<div id='poem_1236648' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236648' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236648?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋山居图<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴九年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年8月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236648")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236648_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236648'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236648'>建炎初载秋八月，钱塘营卒婴城作乱，官军四集矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236648_comment'></div>临川王叔毅为新城令，提乡兵来，旗帜精明，号令甚武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236648_comment'></div>一日，服短后衣，投刀入真承祖寨，陈攻打破贼策，尤觉眉目有英气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236648_comment'></div>是时，坐上见所持湖山形势，水墨写成，自云戏笔也，浓淡远迩，历历可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236648_comment'></div>予始知叔毅善画，傲睨古人，胸中略无一点尘土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236648_comment'></div>后十二年，青社赵无量通守晋安，出示叔毅所图《山居》，开卷恍然，殆前身<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1236648", 1236648, "Clauses/25/Comments/1")'>辋川</span>、今代龙眠欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236648_comment'></div>念与无量、叔毅为齐年故人，各已四十有九，齿发向衰，而萍蓬无定，颇欲挹此图，区处住山活计，庶几如对晤语，无量岂亦有意耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236648_comment'></div>此段因缘，要当为我举似叔毅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236648_comment'></div>傥问予山居之乐，则未必在二子下风也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236648_comment'></div>绍兴己未中秋，芦川老隐跋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1236648_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年9月</a>　九月，新任福建路安抚大使兼知福州张浚寿辰，上诗以贺。作品：《张丞相生朝二十韵》<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　是年，与范才元唱和。作品：《范才元参议求酒于延平使君邀予同赋谨次其韵》《次韵范才元中秋不见月》《奉简才元探梅有作兼怀旧游》《才元思如泉涌愈和愈好晨兴遣骑扣门披衣疾读走笔再酬严韵》《冬夜痴坐似闻才元作集有日矣因和前韵奉呈》《范才元道中杂兴》《浣溪沙•范才元自酿色香如玉直与绿萼梅同调宛然京洛气味也因名曰萼绿梅春且作一首谚以窃尝为吹笙云》<div href='/Writing/107907?labeling=true' target='_blank'>雍熙堂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_107907")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_107907_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_107907'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_107907'>鼎彝勋业推元老，文采风流及后昆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_107907_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_107907'>家世从来耐官职，百年犹见典刑存<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_107907_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_107907'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_107907_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_107907'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_107907_0'>⑴ 宋胡仔《苕溪渔隐丛话》前集卷五四　《苕溪渔隐丛话》：余宣和间居泗上，于王周士处见张仲宗诗一卷，因借录之。后三十年，于钱塘与仲宗同馆谷，初方识之。余因戏谓仲宗曰：“三十年前，已识公于诗卷中。”仲宗请余举其诗，渠皆不能记，殆如隔世，反从余求之。向伯恭，仲宗之舅也。仲宗有《香林九咏》，其间《雍熙堂》诗云云。</div></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236681_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236681'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236681'>一且谓吾仕耶，毁冠裂冕，与世阔疏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236681_comment'></div>一且谓吾隐耶，垂手入廛，与人为徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236681_comment'></div>愧姓名之未能变，何形容之犹可图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236681_comment'></div>颇欲治货殖兮，方陶朱公不足；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236681_comment'></div>聊复啖杞菊兮，视天随生有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236681_comment'></div>行年五十矣，虽髭发粗黑，然田庐皆无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236681_comment'></div>陶陶兀兀，遇饮辄醉，著枕即寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236681_comment'></div>一念不生，万事不理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236681_comment'></div>至于酒醒梦觉，则又大笑而起，摩腹叩齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236681_comment'></div>孰不睥睨曰：「此老真甚愚」！</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1236681_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年3月</a>　三月，闻张浚复特进而奉启以贺。作品：《贺张丞相浚复特进启》<div id='poem_1236615' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236615' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236615?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺张丞相浚复特进启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236615")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236615_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236615'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236615'>申命九年，升华一品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236615_comment'></div>望著群公之表，班联三事之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236615_comment'></div>宠数荐加，忠猷益壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236615_comment'></div>恭以某官经纶密勿，蚤感遇于风云；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236615_comment'></div>燮理协和，尝寅亮于天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236615_comment'></div>出入将相，勤劳国家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236615_comment'></div>眷是殊勋，临兹巨屏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236615_comment'></div>体貌优而均逸，威令信而底宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236615_comment'></div>屈御侮折冲之谋，施坐啸画诺之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236615_comment'></div>元戎十乘，聊作镇于瓯闽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236615_comment'></div>泰阶六符，忽腾辉于宸极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236615_comment'></div>思万方之助顺，转一气于洪钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236615_comment'></div>允属具瞻，式昭简注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236615_comment'></div>服苍玉之佩，宛是青毡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236615_comment'></div>歌绣裳之诗，定归赤舄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236615_comment'></div>佐君王之神武，拯涂炭之生灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236615_comment'></div>驾驭英雄，削平祸乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236615_comment'></div>霆惊寇盗以必灭，电扫寰区而尽收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236615_comment'></div>卜中兴年，密迩上元之甲子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236615_comment'></div>趋行在所，雍容今代之崇臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236615_comment'></div>社稷之盘石再安，带砺之山河永赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236615_comment'></div>某自嗟旅次，徒调制词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236615_comment'></div>企踵恩门，莫厕登龙之后；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236615_comment'></div>驰心广厦，尤增贺燕之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236615_comment'></div>欣幸交深，敷宣罔罄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236615_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1236615_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年</a>　是春，筑鸥盟轩成，以诗书怀。作品：《次友人书怀》<div id='poem_107956' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_107956' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/107956?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次友人书怀<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_107956")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_107956_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_107956'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_107956'>此生无意入修门，粗饱鸡豚短褐温。<div id='poem_sentence_0_107956_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_107956'>卜筑几椽临水屋，经营数亩傍山园。<div id='poem_sentence_1_107956_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' showDetail'><a href='/Writing/108166?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宝鼎现 筠翁李似之作此词见招，因赋其事，使歌之者想像风味，如到山中也</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年</a>　以诗贺新任福建安抚大使程迈生辰。作品：《福帅生朝二首》<div id='poem_108052' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108052' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年</a>　中秋后，尝陪程迈宴饮，有词。作品：《水调歌头•陪福帅燕集口占以受官奴》<div id='poem_108130' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108130' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_108130_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_108130'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_108130'>缥缈九重阁，壮观在人间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_108130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_108130'>凉飙乍起，四围晴黛入阑干。<div id='poem_sentence_1_108130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_108130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_108130'>为寿一樽欢。<div id='poem_sentence_4_108130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
