ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年10月17日</a>　在连江，会遇朱松。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年</a>　应连江知县阮圭之请，作《福州连江县潘渡石桥记》<div id='poem_1236666' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236666' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236666?labeling=true' target='_blank'>福州连江县潘渡石桥记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236666")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236666_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236666'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236666'>闽中统八州之地，重山复岭，绵亘联属，而傍海城邑，亦居其半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236666_comment'></div>大抵溪壑之交会，潮汐之吐吞，或汇为深渊，或激为奔湍，必曰蛟螭窟穴存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236666_comment'></div>设有舟楫，乘险可虞，恶少椎埋，得以邀留行旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236666_comment'></div>自夏徂秋，飓母飘烈，瞬息暴至，固使人惴慄震悼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236666_comment'></div>一旦雷雨晦冥，莫辨咫尺，凡问津者，皆病涉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236666_comment'></div>皇朝嘉祐间，莆阳蔡公君谟守温陵，始作石桥万安渡，雄盛冠于东南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236666_comment'></div>丰碑岿然，大书深刻，邦人至今祠之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236666_comment'></div>其墨本流传，常在人耳目，自尔所至，多取规模。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236666_comment'></div>然世间假修头陀行之流，往往藉此为奸，利囊橐，徒费岁月，迄无成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236666_comment'></div>如连江潘渡，本以姓著，先是里人林道夫等权舆其事，岁在乙卯，历四载，仅能凿石庀材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236666_comment'></div>已而僧资逸辈嗣之，既再期，会计所醵金共不满二百万，皆废于索址，随筑屡毁，沙水荡潏，涨落崩腾，莫之御也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236666_comment'></div>道夫、资逸心志俱怠，辄弃去，又再期矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236666_comment'></div>前安抚使程进道适由永嘉移镇此邦，壬戌春二月也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236666_comment'></div>渡有候馆，公少休焉，谓此渡实罗源、宁德、长溪三邑涂所自出，而车马如浙东、广右者络绎往来，念当积潦之患，与夫向所谓凡问津病涉者，诚不可无桥以济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236666_comment'></div>锐意是举，召知县事阮侯朝瑞，俾经营之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236666_comment'></div>侯思虑精密，善揣摩，用钩距，略不畀付胥徒，阴择所治号能住持僧数人者董其役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236666_comment'></div>又得净安之思显，授以程度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236666_comment'></div>思显坚忍通练，出纳惟谨，而畏督责，常踧踖救过不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236666_comment'></div>予窃怪侯乃能从容三尺之间，独仰众人乐从，有成如此，不其难哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236666_comment'></div>然则是非毁誉，果可卜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236666_comment'></div>时当终更，夤缘以书来，求予为之记甚力，予将何辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236666_comment'></div>姑缀缉本末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236666_comment'></div>阮侯名圭，朝瑞盖其字，是亦莆阳人云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1236666_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年</a>　是年，汪藻知泉州以启致贺。作品：《贺泉州汪内翰藻启》<div id='poem_1236620' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236620' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236620?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺泉州汪内翰藻启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236620")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236620_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236620'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236620'>光奉制恩，宠移会府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236620_comment'></div>商飙肃驶，壮徒御以遄征；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236620_comment'></div>海气澄开，饬阴灵而奔卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236620_comment'></div>谅诹辰之筮吉，宜考履以膺祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236620_comment'></div>恭惟某官道总四科，材通八凯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236620_comment'></div>专良史之直笔，东观著书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236620_comment'></div>掞大册以高文，北门视草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236620_comment'></div>爰分符竹，屡拥驷车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236620_comment'></div>推为二千石吏师，懋乃五百年贤业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236620_comment'></div>尊儒稽古，决事据经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236620_comment'></div>治行必以首称，威声闻而股慄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236620_comment'></div>黄堂坐啸，方来传德政之碑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236620_comment'></div>皂盖行春，所至立生祠之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236620_comment'></div>古由太守，入拜上公，载瞻当宁之眷贤，式际中兴之盛典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236620_comment'></div>某夙蒙知遇，自愧迂愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236620_comment'></div>思远引于旧山，未能毕娶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236620_comment'></div>顾滞留于逆旅，犹及扫门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236620_comment'></div>傥加三沐三熏之仁，遂忘一贵一贱之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236620_comment'></div>获依巨荫，辄叙牢愁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236620_comment'></div>伫接武于宾阶，敢通名于记室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236620_comment'></div>永言欣幸，实倍等夷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1236620_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年2月22日</a>　居福州。二月二十二日，与富直柔游，富为之题跋。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年2月</a>　二月晦，叶份与游，并为之题跋。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年6月1日</a>　六月初一，在福州与叶梦得游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年8月15日</a>　中秋，叶梦得在福州宴客，芦川、富直柔皆与焉。作品：《念奴娇•代洛滨次石林韵》<div id='poem_108167' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108167' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/108167?labeling=true' target='_blank'>念奴娇<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>代洛滨次石林韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年8月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_108167")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_108167_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_108167'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_108167'>吴淞初冷，记垂虹南望，残日西沈。<div id='poem_sentence_0_108167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_108167'>秋入青冥三万顷，蟾影吞尽湖阴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_108167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_108167'>玉斧为谁，冰轮如许，宫阙想寒深。<div id='poem_sentence_2_108167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_108167'>人间奇观，古今豪士悲吟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_108167_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_108167'>苍弁丹颊仙翁，淮山风露底，曾赋幽寻。<div id='poem_sentence_4_108167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_108167'>老去专城仍好客，时拥歌吹登临。<div id='poem_sentence_5_108167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_108167'>坐揖龙江，举杯相属，桂子落波心。<div id='poem_sentence_6_108167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_108167'>一声猿啸，醉来虚籁千林。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_108167_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年12月</a>　年底，有诗贺叶梦得寿辰。作品：《叶少蕴生朝》<div id='poem_108068' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108068' class='poemTitle id='poem_sentence_5_108068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_108068'>中开香火祠殊庭，石林高卧忧苍生。<div id='poem_sentence_6_108068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年9月</a>　九月，故人薛弼移帅福州，作启以贺。作品：《贺薛帅移闽启》<div id='poem_1236625' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236625' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236625?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺薛帅移闽启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236625")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236625_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236625'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236625'>肃膺明制，宠易近藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236625_comment'></div>舍五岭之炎方，临三山之乐土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236625_comment'></div>旌旄改色，鼓角增雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236625_comment'></div>士论所归，宸恩尤重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236625_comment'></div>恭惟某官天资浑厚，德宇粹温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236625_comment'></div>藏利器以变通，蕴远猷而康济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236625_comment'></div>宜处名卿钜公之位，固多君子长者之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236625_comment'></div>事不辞难，蚤飞腾于要路；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236625_comment'></div>人惟求旧，爰登用于熙朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236625_comment'></div>尝抚荆渚之上游，荐镇赣川之剧郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236625_comment'></div>懋昭异绩，益著先声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236625_comment'></div>兹闻成命之初颁，式慰群情之素服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236625_comment'></div>寇攘欲殄，师旅方屯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236625_comment'></div>咸责备于韬钤，伫召还于枢筦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236625_comment'></div>非徒报政，当见策勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236625_comment'></div>某自弃蒿莱，久栖云壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236625_comment'></div>从大将军之幕府，曩虽预乎同僚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236625_comment'></div>望都督府之戟门，念将陪于下客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236625_comment'></div>讵敢恃金兰之契，聊复伸桑梓之恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236625_comment'></div>欣幸交深，敷陈罔既。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236625_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1236625_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236682'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236682'>这痴汉，没思算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236682_comment'></div>初乏田园，却懒仕宦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236682_comment'></div>辨得所向方圆，未尝敢做崖岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236682_comment'></div>只用两仆肩舆，不羡傥来轩冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236682_comment'></div>投閒二十馀年，善类干烦殆遍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236682_comment'></div>好之者彻底信其真贫，恶之者岂免遭他点检。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236682_comment'></div>要当毕娶杜门，自断此生忧患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236682_comment'></div>罢去谒府参官，一等著衣吃饭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236682_comment'></div>休拈翰墨文章，说甚安危治乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236682_comment'></div>就使立事赴功，决定违条碍贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236682_comment'></div>个中人，高著眼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236682_comment'></div>方瞳绿发照青春，期与飞仙游汗漫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236682_comment'></div>现此风狂道士身，长庚晓月聊相伴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236682_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1236682_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a id='poem_content_1236697'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236697'>旧岁旱暵甚广，诸方乃大例关堂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236697_comment'></div>今春饥馑异常，此地亦随时贵籴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236697_comment'></div>维康僧之香火，号圣迹之道场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236697_comment'></div>初无田畴，悉仰檀越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236697_comment'></div>钟鱼之响已间断，粥饭之缘将落空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236697_comment'></div>是念贫女一钱，瓣心即同瓣贡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236697_comment'></div>稍宽斋肠三篾，知恩方解报恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236697_comment'></div>欲种善因，势须猛舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236697_comment'></div>莫看居士面，且试老婆心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236697_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1236697_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>　有与赵元功唱和诗。作品：《次韵赵元功赠李季言之什》《次韵元功之什》《次韵元功才友道中见赠因以解嘲》<div id='poem_107976' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_107976' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1151&endYear=1151')">1151年1月1日</a>　正月初一，作生朝醮词。作品：《辛未岁本命生朝醮词》<br /></div><div class='label1' id='a180198cf0ee40d29483192c9006e964_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a180198cf0ee40d29483192c9006e964");'><span id='a180198cf0ee40d29483192c9006e964_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年</a>，64岁</div><div id='a180198cf0ee40d29483192c9006e964' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>九月，回闽中，为王叔济作《亦乐居士集序》<div id='poem_1236631' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236631' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236631?labeling=true' target='_blank'>亦乐居士文集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1154年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236631")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236631_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236631'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236631'>文章名世，自有渊源，殆与天地元气同流，可以斡旋造化，关键顾在人所钟禀及师授为如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236631_comment'></div>譬犹一身，五官百骸，各随形模，万态不同，至于上下左右，则难以倒置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236631_comment'></div>必也精神发挥，乃中仪矩，不然，土木偶尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236631_comment'></div>前辈尝云：诗句当法子美，其他述作无出退之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236631_comment'></div>韩、杜门庭，风行水上，自然成文，俱名活法，金声玉振，正如吾夫子集大成，盖确论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236631_comment'></div>国初，儒宗杨、刘数公，沿袭五代衰陋，号西昆体，未能超诣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236631_comment'></div>庐陵欧阳文忠公初得退之诗文于汉东弊箧故书中，爱其言辨意深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236631_comment'></div>已而官于洛，乃与尹师鲁讲习，文风丕变，寖近古矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236631_comment'></div>未几，文安先生苏明允起于西蜀，父子兄弟俱文忠公门下士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236631_comment'></div>东坡之门，又得山谷，檃栝诗律，于是少陵句法大振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236631_comment'></div>如张文潜、晁无咎、秦少游、陈无己之流，相望辈出，世不乏才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236631_comment'></div>是岂无渊源而然耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236631_comment'></div>故尚书户部侍郎豫章王公承可，人品高妙，其文章深造少陵阃域，一时声名，籍甚荐绅间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236631_comment'></div>惜乎天不假年，位未称德，善类衋伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236631_comment'></div>后六年，公之第三子湑叔济手裒先人平生所著，总若干篇，离为六卷，名曰《亦乐居士文集》，子职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236631_comment'></div>叔济贤而有文，克世其家，一日属予序之，将镂板传于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236631_comment'></div>予晚生，虽不及见东坡、山谷，而少时在江西，实从东湖徐公师川授以句法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236631_comment'></div>东湖，山谷甥也，贰卿视东湖里中丈人行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236631_comment'></div>东湖昂藏严毅，不妄许可，集中多有赠答，斯已可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236631_comment'></div>然而今代鸿儒，以文鸣要路，能轩轾人者颇多；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236631_comment'></div>叔济不他求，反取信于退閒无闻之老，何耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236631_comment'></div>得非以皇祐中<span class='inlineComment2'>（原本阙四字。）</span>与先祖同年进士，迨宣和初，少师公帅广陵，予以年家孙展拜床下，复齿长贰卿三岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236631_comment'></div>辈行既同，情义不啻手足，景服言行之详，诚莫予若也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236631_comment'></div>叔济用予芜颣之语，俾冠编帙，获托名不朽，幸矣，尚何敢辞！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236631_comment'></div>贰卿在朝廷，则献纳论思，书于史官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236631_comment'></div>在方镇，则抚绥智略，碑于德政，固不待予言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236631_comment'></div>姑推其渊源所自来，追古作者如此，后之君子必有处之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236631_comment'></div>绍兴二十四年九月晦日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1236631_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>王叔济赴临安任职，芦川在闽为之送行。作品：《临江仙•送王叔济》<div id='poem_108185' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108185' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/108185?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临江仙<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>送王叔济</a><span class='authorDate'>（1154年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_108185")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_108185_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_108185'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_108185'>玉立清标消晚暑，胸中一段冰壶。<div id='poem_sentence_0_108185_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_108185'>画船归去醉歌姝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_108185_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_108185'>微云收未尽，残月炯如初。<div id='poem_sentence_2_108185_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_108185'>鸳鹭行间催阔步，秋来乘兴凫趋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_108185_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_108185'>烦君为我问西湖。<div id='poem_sentence_4_108185_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_108185'>不知疏影畔，许我结茅无。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_108185_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
古田
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4e7a63b0a2e74ddd81838fc011da1da9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4e7a63b0a2e74ddd81838fc011da1da9");'><span id='4e7a63b0a2e74ddd81838fc011da1da9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>，50岁</div><div id='4e7a63b0a2e74ddd81838fc011da1da9' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>夏四月初五，自号真隐山人。在水口精舍有跋文。作品：《跋少游帖》《跋苏黄门帖》<div id='poem_1236639' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236639' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236639")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236639_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236639'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236639'>吾家顷岁藏少游《访龙井辩才师行记》手藁，字画遒媚，深有二王楷法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236639_comment'></div>建炎丁未，寓居西湖，秋八月，兵乱亡去，今踰一纪矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236639_comment'></div>忽见史侯持正所携帖，念之惘然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236639_comment'></div>绍兴庚申初夏五日，真隐山人书于水口精舍。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1236639_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1236640' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236640' </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236640")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236640_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236640'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236640'>苏黄门顷自海康归许下，安居云久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236640_comment'></div>政和二年，晚生犹及识之，衣冠俨古，语简而色庄，真元祐钜公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236640_comment'></div>已而与其外孙文骥德称相遇澶渊，出书帖富甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236640_comment'></div>今观史侯所藏数幅，盖中年笔札也，兵火之馀，岂易得哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236640_comment'></div>是宜什袭，遗诸子孙，不妨模以墨本，流传于世。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1236640_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

id='poem_sentence_6_108214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_108214'>笑傲，且山中宰相，平地蓬莱。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_108214_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='e0b35bce0b17418b870d5565044c633a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e0b35bce0b17418b870d5565044c633a");'><span id='e0b35bce0b17418b870d5565044c633a_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年</a>　芦川送秋香酒给弥逊，同时作《鹤冲天》词并寄，后呈于富直柔。作品：《鹤冲天•呈富枢密》<br /></div><div class='label1' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1148')">1148年2月</a>　与友人过连江宝积寺，有诗题壁。作品：《戊辰春二月晦同栖鸾子送所亲过宝积题壁间》<div id='poem_107947' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_107947' class='poemTitle class='poemContent' id='poem_content_107947'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_107947'>春江因送客，云峤更登临。<div id='poem_sentence_0_107947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_107947'>精舍经行地，征人去住心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_107947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_107947'>猿啼清梦断，花落晓窗阴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_107947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_107947'>胜践成三宿，俱来此意深。<div id='poem_sentence_3_107947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
苏州

<div class='label1' id='77a819e86dfb4470a9b9a31a73b6283a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("77a819e86dfb4470a9b9a31a73b6283a");'><span id='77a819e86dfb4470a9b9a31a73b6283a_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年8月15日</a>　是年秋，游苏州虎丘，有词。作品：《水调歌头•癸酉虎丘中秋》<div id='poem_108127' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108127' class='poemTitle id='poem_title_108127_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_108127'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_108127'>万里冰轮满，千丈玉盘浮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_108127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_108127'>广寒宫殿，西望湖海冷光流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_108127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_108127'>扫尽长空纤翳，散乱疏林清影，风露迫人愁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_108127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_108127'>徐步行歌去，危坐不眠休。<div id='poem_sentence_3_108127_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_108127'>问孤蓬，缘底事，苦淹留。<div id='poem_sentence_4_108127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_108127'>倦游回首，向来云卧两<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_108127", 108127, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>星周</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_108127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_108127'>此夜此生长好，明月明年何处，归兴在南州。<div id='poem_sentence_6_108127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_108127'>老境一伧父，异县四中秋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_108127_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年</a>　游吴越，有词。作品：《水调歌头》（平日几经过）《水调歌头》（雨断翻惊浪）<div id='poem_108128' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108128' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_108128'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_108128'>平日几经过，重到更留连。<div id='poem_sentence_0_108128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_108128'>黄尘乌帽，觉来眼界忽醒然。<div id='poem_sentence_1_108128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_108128'>坐见如云秋稼，莫问鸡虫<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_4_108128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_108128'>胸中万顷空旷，清夜炯无眠。<div id='poem_sentence_5_108128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_108128'>要识世间闲处，自有樽前深趣，且唱钓鱼船。<div id='poem_sentence_6_108128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_108128'>调鼎他年事，妙手看<span class='link' id='poem_title_108133' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/108133?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_108133_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_108133'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_108133'>雨断翻惊浪，山暝拥归云。<div id='poem_sentence_0_108133_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_108133'>麦秋天气，聊泛征棹泊江村。<div id='poem_sentence_1_108133_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_108133'>不羡腰间金印，却爱吾庐高枕，无事闭柴门。<div id='poem_sentence_2_108133_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_108133'>搔首烟波上，老去任乾坤。<div id='poem_sentence_3_108133_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_108133'>白纶巾，玉麈尾，一杯春。<div id='poem_sentence_4_108133_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_108133'>性灵陶冶，我辈犹要个中人。<div id='poem_sentence_5_108133_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_108133'>莫变姓名吴市，且向渔樵争席，与世共浮沉。<div id='poem_sentence_6_108133_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_108133'>目送飞鸿去，何用画麒麟。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_108133_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='b901e311d8c3434da18873ce10ae52b8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b901e311d8c3434da18873ce10ae52b8");'><span id='b901e311d8c3434da18873ce10ae52b8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1160')">1159-1160年</a>，69-70岁</div><div id='b901e311d8c3434da18873ce10ae52b8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年</a>　夏秋间，在苏州为陈正同校订《了堂先生文集》成。作品：《跋了堂先生文集》<div id='poem_1236632' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236632' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236632?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋了堂先生文集</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236632")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236632_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236632'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236632'>某愚且戆，不学无术，卒老于行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236632_comment'></div>然少时有志，从前辈长者游，担簦竭蹶，不舍昼夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236632_comment'></div>宣和庚子春，拜忠肃公于庐山之南，陪侍杖屦，幽寻云烟水石间者累月，与闻前言往行，商榷古今治乱成败，夜分乃就寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236632_comment'></div>先生尝谓孺子可教，赐以大父手泽，题跋曰：「为士而能尊其祖，为子而能干父之蛊，此可久之习也，辞采灿然，足以有誉于世矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236632_comment'></div>某书绅，佩服终身弗忘，且刊之碑版，永藏于家，贻训子孙，墨犹未乾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236632_comment'></div>顾某何人，乃获先生知遇期待如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236632_comment'></div>兹者又辱次对，贰卿崇笃先契，不鄙荒唐，容许校雠《了堂文集》，得非目前贤士大夫及识先生者所存无几耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236632_comment'></div>于是自夏涉秋，手加审订，凡字画之讹舛，伦序之失次，是非之去取，分部卷帙，各适其当，具如别录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236632_comment'></div>傥或其说可采，邵州旧版于理当捐，且并刻《易说》、谏藁，合而为一，始克尽善，庶几后学知所师承，不为异端所惑，于道岂小补也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236632_comment'></div>昔韩文公为唐室一代儒宗，而门人李汉、赵德实为之编次，且序冠其首，遂托名以垂不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236632_comment'></div>某晚生，固不敢序先生之文，幸从事于编次，似无愧于李、赵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236632_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236632_comment'></div>自王氏网罗六艺，断以己意，力行新法，变乱旧章，天下遂多事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236632_comment'></div>已而子婿兄弟，表里祖述，遗祸无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236632_comment'></div>先生独知尊尧，爱君忧国，先见之明，肇于欲萌，逆料其弊，甚于中的。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236632_comment'></div>视之若雠敌，甘心犯难，虽百谪濒九死而弗悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236632_comment'></div>孟轲氏曰：「<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1236632", 1236632, "Clauses/78/Comments/1")'>富贵不能淫</span>，贫贱不能移，威武不能屈，此之谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1236632", 1236632, "Clauses/81/Comments/1")'>大丈夫</span>」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236632_comment'></div>又曰：「我善养吾浩然之气，至大至刚，以直养而无害，则塞乎天地之间」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236632_comment'></div>合而言之，愚于先生平日立朝行己，信无疑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236632_comment'></div>百世之下，凛凛英气，义形于色，如砥柱之屹颓波，如泰华之插穹昊，如万折必东之水，如百炼不变之金，舍吾先生其谁哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236632_comment'></div>死而不亡者，予于先生见之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1236632_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　春，在苏州，有《上平江陈侍郎十绝》诗。<div id='poem_108066' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108066' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_108066")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_108066_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_108066'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_108066'>了堂先生古遗直，贬剥私史专尊尧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_108066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_108066'>二蔡怀奸首<span class='inlineComment2'>（原校：一作力）</span>排击，始终大节不同朝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_107859_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_107865' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_107865' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/107865?labeling=true' id='poem_title_107861_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_107861'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_107861'>酒酣怒发上冲冠，四十年前庐阜南。<div id='poem_sentence_0_107861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_107861'>杖履周旋痛开警，为言小子颇尝参。<div id='poem_sentence_1_107861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_996131_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_996131'>经离乱，青山尽处，海角又天涯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_996131_comment'></div></div><br /><div onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_996131", 996131, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>价例</span>，毫发更无差。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_996131_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
吴江

class='authorDate'>（1159年8月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_108178")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_108178_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_108178'>贺方回所作，世间和韵者多矣。余经行松江，何啻百回，念欲下一转语，了无好怀。此来偶有得，当与吾宗椿老子载酒浩歌西湖南山间，写我滞思，二公不可不入社也</div><div id='poem_preface_108178_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_108178'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_108178'>平生百绕<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_108178", 108178, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>垂虹</span>路。<div id='poem_sentence_0_108178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_108178'>看万顷、翻云去。<div id='poem_sentence_1_108178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_108178'>山澹夕晖帆影度。<div id='poem_sentence_2_108178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_108178'>菱歌风断，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_108178", 108178, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>袜罗</span>尘散，总是关情处。<div id='poem_sentence_3_108178_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_108178'>少年陈迹今迟暮。<div id='poem_sentence_4_108178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_108178'>走笔犹能醉时句。<div id='poem_sentence_5_108178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_108178'>花底目成心暗许。<div id='poem_sentence_6_108178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_108178'>旧家春事，觉来客恨，分付疏篷雨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_108178_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
嘉兴（嘉兴府）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5af1e551396f464a889ffc7bf9c3712e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5af1e551396f464a889ffc7bf9c3712e");'><span id='5af1e551396f464a889ffc7bf9c3712e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>，67岁</div><div id='5af1e551396f464a889ffc7bf9c3712e' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>五月中旬，在嘉兴与苏庭藻游。作品：《跋苏诏君楚语后》《跋苏庭藻隶书后二篇》《走笔次廷藻韵二绝》《西江月•和苏廷藻》《跋苏诏君赠王道士诗后》《苏廷藻画赞》<div id='poem_1236659' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236659' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236659?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋苏诏君楚语后<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二十七年五月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236659")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236659_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236659'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236659'>《风》、《雅》之变，始有《离骚》，与《诗》六义相表里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236659_comment'></div>比兴虽多，然卒皆正而不淫，哀而不怨，宜乎古今推屈、宋为盟主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236659_comment'></div>后之数子，如《九怀》、《九叹》、《七发》、《七启》之类，著意摹仿，未免重复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236659_comment'></div>姑置工拙如何，大槩开卷使人易倦，良由轨辙一律，窃窃然追逐前贤步武间，心殚力疲，不能跳脱翰墨畦径，良可恨尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236659_comment'></div>观吾养直所作，摅发己意，肆而不拘，凡所形容，不蕲合于屈、宋，政自超诣，殆不可企及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236659_comment'></div>此章赠别从周者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236659_comment'></div>顷在东都，一日，陈去非、吕居仁诸公同予避暑资圣阁，以「二仪清浊还高下，三伏炎蒸定有无」分韵赋诗，会者适十四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236659_comment'></div>从周诗颇佳，为诸公印可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236659_comment'></div>然则阮嗣宗喜仲容，又常曰「吾不如与阿戎谈」，方之养直，惓惓如此，不为过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236659_comment'></div>从周后养直数载云亡，其子庭藻有志古学，手抄《离骚》，成诵不辍，且求为乃翁跋所藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236659_comment'></div>顾家有哲匠，但熟读数百过，何患落笔不名世耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236659_comment'></div>芦川老人书于槜李弭棹亭中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236659_comment'></div>丁丑仲夏望日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1236659_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1236660' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236660' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236660?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋苏庭藻隶书后<span class='inlineComment2'>（一　绍兴二十七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236660")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236660_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236660'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236660'>士抱美质，必加砥砺，以立廉隅，始克有成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236660_comment'></div>若挟所长，傲形于色，掩其美矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236660_comment'></div>《传》不云乎：「虽有周公之才之美，使骄且吝，其馀不足观也已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236660_comment'></div>庭藻，润公五世孙，种种落笔，便有见处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236660_comment'></div>要是兰方茁，知其为国香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236660_comment'></div>但年少气豪，高视万物之表，太露圭角，伤锋犯手，未免遭人诋訾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236660_comment'></div>能痛锄傲慢，善择交友，涵养器业，且饱读古人书，自然左右逢原，岂易量耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236660_comment'></div>予及从景谟宗丞公游，景谟宗丞公常呼予在辈行，此言未为过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236660_comment'></div>一日，故人凌世高出示庭藻隶字甚古，把玩久之，可喜亦可念，因书于卷末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236660_comment'></div>廷藻其志之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236660_comment'></div>丁丑结制前九日，老隐跋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1236660_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1236661' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236661' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236661?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋苏庭藻隶书后<span class='inlineComment2'>（二　绍兴二十七年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236661")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236661_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236661'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236661'>近世隶学，罕师西汉笔法，易入八分者，无他，盖习《魏受禅碑》，一落畦径，便不可医，此手法大病也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236661_comment'></div>庭藻始留心作隶字，便得拙意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236661_comment'></div>开卷未论是非，而气象奇古，已觉度胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236661_comment'></div>积之岁月，当过人十数等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236661_comment'></div>绍兴丁丑夏四月己未，老隐云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1236661_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_107877' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_107877' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/107877?labeling=true' target='_blank'>走笔次廷藻韵二绝<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_107877")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_107877_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_107877'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_107877'>风雨声中过半春，泥深郊水阻游人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_107877_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_107877'>老夫不出浑闲事，但觉年来白发新。<div id='poem_sentence_1_107877_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_107877'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_107877_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_107876' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_107876' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/107876?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年5月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_107876_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_107876'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_107876'>小苏一物绝风流，竹杖芒鞋爱讨幽。<div id='poem_sentence_0_107876_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_107876'>招隐归来吐佳句，何时一笑共重游。<div id='poem_sentence_1_107876_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_107876'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_107876_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_108157' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_108157' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/108157?labeling=true' target='_blank'>西江月 和苏庭藻</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_108157")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_108157_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_108157'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_108157'>小阁劣容老子，北窗仍递南风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_108157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_108157'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_108157", 108157, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>维摩丈室</span>久空空。<div id='poem_sentence_1_108157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_108157'>不与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_108157", 108157, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>散花</span>同梦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_108157_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_108157'>且作太真游戏，未甘<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_108157", 108157, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>金粟</span>龙钟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_108157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_108157'>怜君病后颊颧隆。<div id='poem_sentence_4_108157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_108157'>识取<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_108157", 108157, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>小儿</span>戏弄。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_108157_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1236658' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236658' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236658?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋苏诏君赠王道士诗后<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二十七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236658")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236658_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236658'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236658'>文章盖自造化窟中来，元气融结胸次，古今谓之活法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236658_comment'></div>所以血脉贯穿，首尾俱应，如常山蛇势；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236658_comment'></div>又如风行水上，自然成文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236658_comment'></div>又如优人作戏，出场要须留笑，退思有味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236658_comment'></div>非独为文，凡涉世建立，同一关键。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236658_comment'></div>吾友养直平生得禅家自在三昧，片言只字，无一点尘埃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236658_comment'></div>宇宙山川，云烟草木，千变万态，尽在笔端，何曾气索？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236658_comment'></div>此篇顷见别本尚馀一联云「故岁去超忽，来日俄趣装」，方入断章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236658_comment'></div>虽曰达人大观，然太涉悲戚，殆似鬼中太白，真语谶也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236658_comment'></div>养直下世，今将一纪矣，九原可复作耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236658_comment'></div>读之怆然，并为从周之子庭藻记之卷末，庶几风流不泯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236658_comment'></div>绍兴丁丑夏至后七日，芦川老人书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1236658_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1236679' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236679' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236679?labeling=true' target='_blank'>苏庭藻画赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25448, "宋", "张元干", "poem_title_1236679")'>张元干</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236679_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236679'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236679'>贤公孙而乐为寒士生涯，佳少年而慕用前辈风味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236679_comment'></div>盖名驹在闲，已有千里之足；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236679_comment'></div>于菟堕地，便有食牛之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236679_comment'></div>天乎早孤，自立于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236679_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236679_comment'></div>抗志患不高，其高常失于绝物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236679_comment'></div>阅书患不广，其广或滞于未通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236679_comment'></div>必也裹阳秋于皮里，吞云梦于胸中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236679_comment'></div>是宜尚友古之人，道何虑不挺挺然祖风？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236679_comment'></div>充乎大者自可以华其国，用其小者亦足以美厥躬。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1236679_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
